There are also standard robots in hotels now~

The main reason for coming to this hotel is the beach. It is a beautiful white sand beach, which is very photogenic. We said goodbye reluctantly at 4:30 when the sea breeze started to get cold. I saw that there are many facilities in the water park here, and there is also a large swimming pool, which is currently closed. It can be seen that there must be a lot of people in summer.

The hotel package includes the Five Kingdoms Hot Springs (four are open) and the children's park nearby, which is a 15-minute walk away. The Five Kingdoms Hot Springs is very large, with many hot springs, mostly outdoors, open until very late, but it will be a bit cold to walk around after dark. There are also saunas, fish therapy pools, etc. The Italian Pavilion also has children's amusement facilities, and the Thai Pavilion has a good infinity pool. Only the Japanese Pavilion is open for catering at night, and the price is not expensive, so it‚Äôs okay to eat casually.

The children's park is very large, including the regular park on the first floor, the trampoline world upstairs, the outdoor amusement area on the first floor, the indoor mechanical equipment next to the park on the first floor, and an indoor sand-digging pool on the first floor that is hard to find!

The regular park is so-so. The hollow mesh tube made my legs cramp... I have never seen such a hard one... The super-large ocean ball pool + slide on the periphery is quite shocking.

The trampoline world is quite good. My son and I played for half an hour, but it can be seen that the equipment is a bit old. One of the doors passing by the elevator smells of urine... The hygiene needs attention.

The weather is cold, so I didn't play the outdoor carousel and pendulum. I played VR and rotating airplanes. They were all in charge of an employee aunt. The aunt was very nice. We had a double ticket and allowed our family of three to play together. The ocean world is too exciting! I also played four themes such as dinosaurs. I stopped because my eyes were a little uncomfortable.

The sand-digging pool is deep inside. We almost missed it. There are very few people. The sand is made of cassia seeds or some herbs. It is fragrant and clean. The area is large, and parents can sit on the periphery to watch.

During the stay, an incident occurred in the children's park. The girl at the front desk said that she couldn't find my guest information, so she asked me to buy tickets for one adult and one child. I always remembered that the accommodation package I bought included tickets for two adults and one child, and I confirmed that it was indeed included in the order, so I asked the housekeeper after the stay. Finally, after a series of twists and turns, the hotel manager helped me refund the tickets.

There is a special area for fireworks outside the hotel. We set off fireworks together at night and watched many big bosses' rich and colorful fireworks for free. You can also enjoy the fireworks show of the local tyrants outside the window and corridor~

I was skeptical and there is no better choice, so come and try it! It took 2 hours to drive from Shanghai and arrived at 2 o'clock. Although there were many people in the hotel, we still checked in in advance. The housekeeper Xiao Qin was very enthusiastic and the service was very thoughtful. We were only going to stay for one day, but we didn't have time to play all the games in the hotel package, so we decided to stay for another night at midnight, but we ran out of room. So next time, be sure to book a 2-day stay package. According to our 3-day play experience, to help you sort out, there are mainly 3 play items for children: Bihai Yinsha, Wuguo Hot Spring Pavilion, and Le World Children's World. Some of these items are offered if you stay in a hotel. It is recommended to play World or Wuguo Hot Springs in the afternoon. We were inexperienced at the beginning and felt that the hot springs were not much fun in summer. We slowly swallowed them at 7 o'clock in the evening, but the baby didn't want to come out after playing in it. Next time, be sure to arrange a whole afternoon to soak in it. The children of Le World can buy the jumping ticket. It is suitable for playing during the day and can be played all day. The bracelet can be entered unlimited times on the same day, so this arrangement is more reasonable on the last day, and you can continue to play after checking out. The blue sea and silver sand can be arranged after dinner, not so dry. As shown in the picture without the filter, it is really a blue sea, and you can see the sea in only 2-3 days in the future. The weather was good and I saw the sunset for several days in a row, but one day it was still pink, so romantic. When I'm not playing in the water, I rent a small electric car and take my children around the resort. The children are also very happy. There are beautiful views everywhere. It feels so good that time is slowing down! Thanks again to the housekeeper Xiao Qin, and I will look for her next time I come.

Heated swimming pool: It is very large, with a professional 50-meter swimming lane and a children's area. The water depth ranges from 1.1 to 1.4 meters. Babies of all ages can have fun, but the water temperature is a bit low, and the air conditioner in the locker room is not turned on enough. The clothes are a little cold, so you can warm up in the wet and dry steam room first.
